00:53:46","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 00:53:46","title":"Coronavirus antibodies may rapidly fade away after infection, according to a new English study","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/coronavirus-study-antibodies-fading-rapidly-after-covid-19-infection-2020-10","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f980ea5f21803001222c254?format=jpeg\" alt=\"coronavirus antibody tests\" height=\"1249\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A member of the medical staff performs a rapid IgG/IgM test for COVID-19 antibody detection on 14 October 14, 2020, in Berlin.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Getty</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The number of people in England with COVID-19 antibodies dropped by more than one-quarter in three months, a new study from Imperial College London found.</li>\n<li>The exact relationship between antibody presence and coronavirus immunity remains unclear, but one study author said falling antibody levels could indicate that population immunity may also be waning.</li>\n<li>\"On the balance of evidence I would say, with what we know for other coronaviruses, it would look as if immunity declines away at the same rate as antibodies decline away,\" Professor Wendy Barclay said.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The presence of coronavirus antibodies dropped by more than a quarter in England in the space of three months this summer, a new large-scale study found. The authors suggest their results may indicate that immunity to the virus within the general population also rapidly faded after the first wave of the pandemic.</p><p>Scientists at Imperial College London found that the share of people who tested positive for antibodies to COVID-19— part of the body's defense against re-infection — fell by 26.5% from June to September: from 6.0% of the population to 4.4%.</p><p>The exact relationship between antibody presence and immunity to the coronavirus remains unclear. <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/long-term-coronavirus-immunity-t-cells-2020-8?r=US&IR=TIR=T\">Although the presence of antibodies suggests a person is likely immune to the virus, that's not the only indicator</a>, and a lack of antibodies in someone who was previously infected may not necessarily mean they've lost their protection.</p><p>According to <a href=\"https://www.cell.com/cell/fulltext/S0092-8674(20)31008-4?rss=yes\">an August study</a>, other layers of protection against reinfection, most notably T cells, are likely also critical in the body's long-term immunity.</p><p>Nonetheless, the authors of the Imperial report suggested that falling levels of antibody prevalence could indicate falling population immunity, given evidence from other human coronaviruses.</p><p>\"We can see the antibodies and we can see them declining and we know that antibodies on their own are quite protective,\" said Professor Wendy Barclay, an author of the report and the head of Infectious Disease at Imperial College London, in comments <a href=\"https://uk.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-britain-antibody/uk-study-finds-evidence-of-waning-antibody-immunity-to-covid-19-over-time-idUKKBN27C009\">cited by Reuters</a>.</p><p>\"On the balance of evidence I would say, with what we know for other coronaviruses, it would look as if immunity declines away at the same rate as antibodies decline away, and that this is an indication of waning immunity at the population level.\"</p><p>Professor Helen Ward, another co-author of the report, <a href=\"https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/health-54696873\">told the BBC</a> that the study suggests \"immunity is waning quite rapidly, we're only three months after our first [round of tests] and we're already showing a 26% decline in antibodies.\"</p><p>Paul Elliott, professor of epidemiology and public health at Imperial College and another of the study's authors, said in a press release emailed to Business Insider:</p><p>\"Our study shows that over time there is reduction in the proportion of people testing positive for antibodies against the virus that causes COVID-19. It remains unclear what level of immunity antibodies provide, or for how long this immunity lasts. If someone tests positive for antibodies, they still need to follow national guidelines including social distancing measures, getting a swab test if they have symptoms and wearing face coverings where required.\"</p><p>The study, which has not yet been peer-reviewed, involved a random selection of 365,000 people over three non-overlapping rounds, who tested themselves for coronavirus antibodies at home between June 20 and September 28 using a finger-prick method.&#160;</p><p>The tests are not full-proof on a person-to-person level. Imperial College says <a href=\"https://www.imperial.ac.uk/news/200713/biggest-study-antibody-finger-prick-tests-identifies/\">the type of tests used</a> were found to \"correctly identify individuals with coronavirus antibodies over 80% of the time while correctly ruling out those who don't in more than 98% of tested individuals.\"</p><p>The smallest decline in antibody levels was observed among 18-24 year olds, where the proportion with antibodies fell by 14.9%. The largest was in those over 75, among whom the proportion fell by 39%.</p><p>For healthcare workers, the proportion of antibodies in the study group did not change over the observation period, which could either reflect they had greater initial exposure to the virus, or could be due to repeated infection, the authors suggested.</p><p>Commenting on the report in a press release emailed to Business Insider, UK Health Minister Lord Bethell said: \"It is also important that everyone knows what this means for them – this study will help in our fight against the virus, but testing positive for antibodies does not mean you are immune to COVID-19.\"<br><br>\"Regardless of the result of an antibody test, everyone must continue to comply with government guidelines including social distancing, self-isolating and getting a test if you have symptoms and always remember Hands, Face, Space.\"</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/coronavirus-study-antibodies-fading-rapidly-after-covid-19-infection-2020-10'>Business Insider</a></div>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Tue, 27 Oct 2020 15:01:34 +0000","feedId":22,"bgimg":"https://i.insider.com/5f980e9c4743a3001216bd49?format=jpeg","linkMd5":"87f0b2c6791f41c011e8c73b6592c40c","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn84@2020_6/2020/10/27/16-54-10-961_54fe83a10ff28865.webp","destWidth":2127,"destHeight":1595,"sourceBytes":173788,"destBytes":173788,"author":"tcolson@businessinsider.com (Thomas Colson)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/5f980ea5f21803001222c254?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn44@2020_1/2020/10/27/16-54-10-141_c9e272e4091376f7.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1603817626709},{"createdTime":"2020-10-28 00:53:46","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 00:53:46","title":"Jack Ma's Ant Group is targeting a record $34 billion IPO. Warren Buffett's Berkshire Hathaway stands to gain from its public debut","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/jack-ma-ant-group-warren-buffett-berkshire-hathaway-stoneco-paytm-2020-10","description":"<p><strong><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f9819324743a3001216bd5e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Warren Buffett and Jack Ma\" height=\"673\" width=\"1346\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Rick Wilking/Reuters; Ruben Sprich/Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></strong></p><ul><li><strong>Alibaba cofounder Jack Ma's Ant Group is gearing up for a record $34 billion IPO.</strong></li><li><strong>Ant owns stakes in two financial-technology companies that also count Warren Buffett's Berkshire Hathaway as an investor.</strong></li><li><strong>Berkshire and Ant both invested in Brazilian e-commerce group StoneCo when it went public in October 2018.</strong></li><li><strong>Buffett's company also bet on the owner of Paytm in August 2018, and Ant owns 30% of the Indian digital-payments specialist's parent company.</strong></li><li><strong><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/international?r=US&IR=TIR=T\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</strong></strong><hr></li></ul><p>Warren Buffett may be looking forward to Ant Group's public debut in the coming weeks, as it promises to pull some of <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/brk-b-stock\">Berkshire Hathaway</a>'s lesser-known investments into the spotlight.</p><p><a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/baba-stock\">Alibaba</a> cofounder Jack Ma spun off Ant from the Chinese e-commerce giant in 2011, but still owns 8.8% of the affiliate. Ant owns Alipay, China's leading online-payments platform. It is <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/ant-group-ipo-billion-largest-ever-jack-ma-alibaba-raise-2020-10-1029721033\">seeking to raise more than $34 billion</a> via a dual listing in Hong Kong and Shanghai, setting the stage for the biggest initial public offering in history.</p><p><strong data-stringify-type=\"bold\"><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">Read more:</em></strong><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">&#160;</em><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/stock-picks-to-buy-companies-beat-q3-earnings-expectations-bofa-2020-10\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-stringify-link=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/stock-picks-to-buy-companies-beat-q3-earnings-expectations-bofa-2020-10\" data-sk=\"tooltip_parent\">BANK OF AMERICA: Buy these 11 underowned stocks ahead of their earnings reports because they're the most likely candidates to beat expectations in the weeks ahead</a></em></p><p>At first glance, Buffett's sprawling conglomerate — which owns scores of businesses such as See's Candies, Geico, and the BNSF railway as well as billion-dollar stakes in Apple, Bank of America, and Coca-Cola — appears to have little in common with Ant, a financial-technology titan.</p><p>However, Berkshire and Ant are both investors in two fintechs, <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/stne-stock\">StoneCo</a> in Brazil and Paytm in India.</p><p>Buffett's company <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/warren-buffett-berkshire-hathaway-snowflake-ipo-110-percent-stoneco-gain-2020-9-1029577322#\">spent about $340 million</a> on StoneCo's shares when it went public in October 2018, giving it a roughly 11% stake in the e-commerce specialist. Ant snapped up $100 million worth of stock at the same time.</p><p>Berkshire also plowed around $360 million into One97 Communications, Paytm's parent company, in August 2018, <a href=\"https://money.cnn.com/2018/08/27/technology/paytm-warren-buffett/index.html\">CNNMoney reported at the time</a>. Ant owns more than 30% of One97, according to its IPO filing, making it a key investor in Paytm, which was <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/paytm-may-use-funding-to-add-new-services-2019-11?r=US&IR=TIR=T\">valued at $16 billion last November</a>.</p><p><strong data-stringify-type=\"bold\"><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">Read more:</em></strong><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">&#160;</em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/chamath-palihapitiya-shares-5-sectors-shaping-long-term-investing-plan-2020-10?r=US&IR=TIR=T\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-stringify-link=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/chamath-palihapitiya-shares-5-sectors-shaping-long-term-investing-plan-2020-10?r=US&IR=TIR=T\" data-sk=\"tooltip_parent\">'I'm basically going to be long growth': Billionaire investor Chamath Palihapitiya has hauled in a 997% return since 2011. He details the 5 sectors shaping his long-term investment playbook.</a></p><p>Buffett famously sticks to businesses he understands and has <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/warre-buffett-berkshire-hathaway-570-million-snowflake-ipo-rare-unicorn-2020-9-1029574925#\">avoided investing in tech companies and IPOs</a> for most of his career, so it's no surprise that he wasn't behind the StoneCo and Paytm bets. Todd Combs, the CEO of Geico and one of Buffett's two portfolio managers, made those wagers.</p><p>Combs also <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/warren-buffett-berkshire-hathaway-snowflake-ipo-stake-800-million-gain-2020-9-1029629868#\">struck the deal</a> for Berkshire to invest $735 million in Snowflake when the cloud-data platform went public in September.</p><p>Ant's mammoth IPO is set to shine a light on its StoneCo and Paytm stakes, and Berkshire's bets on those companies in the process. Given Combs' taste for fintech bets, the two companies may well cross paths again.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/jack-ma-ant-group-warren-buffett-berkshire-hathaway-stoneco-paytm-2020-10'>Business Insider</a></div>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Tue, 27 Oct 2020 13:46:55 +0000","feedId":22,"bgimg":"https://i.insider.com/5f9819424743a3001216bd5f?format=jpeg","linkMd5":"3a7df7dfe8260001f9c12fa857bd7cd6","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn96@2020_6/2020/10/27/16-54-13-975_d12232dde41b34f3.webp","destWidth":1161,"destHeight":870,"sourceBytes":51158,"destBytes":51158,"author":"tmohamed@businessinsider.com (Theron Mohamed)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/5f9819324743a3001216bd5e?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn48@2020_6/2020/10/27/16-54-03-811_bdbaefed5b89e537.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1603817626709},{"createdTime":"2020-10-28 00:53:46","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 00:53:46","title":"A psychological technique my mom taught me when I was a teenager saved my marriage — here's how you can use it to navigate any relationship","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/psychological-technique-mirroring-mom-taught-me-changed-marriage","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e3d8e56d9db1d6381226924?format=jpeg\" alt=\"jersey griggs headshot\" height=\"1747\" width=\"2329\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Jersey Griggs.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Courtesy of Jersey Griggs</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li><a href=\"https://jersey-griggs.github.io/\">Jersey Griggs</a> is a writer specializing in lifestyle topics, who lives on the coast of Maine with her husband and their rescue dog.</li>\n<li>When Griggs was growing up, her mother, a clinical psychologist, would use a conflict-resolution technique called 'mirroring' to make her children feel heard.</li>\n<li>Mirroring is the act of mimicking those around us, which can help establish a rapport between the people communicating.</li>\n<li>When Griggs and her husband found themselves in a silly argument, she suggested mirroring &#8212; and it allowed them to finally understand each other.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Growing up, I didn't always take my mother's advice. But since my mom also happened to be Martha Lauber, a clinical psychologist in private practice on Chicago's North Shore, she invariably had advice to give.</p><p>Which is exactly how mirroring, a technique often employed by therapists, came into my life. During my turbulent teenage years, mirroring was a well-practiced conflict-resolution method in our household.</p><p>Also known as limbic synchrony, mirroring is the act of mimicking those around us. An ingrained social behavior that typically yields positive results, mirroring can help to establish a rapport between humans, with <a href=\"https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC3840169/\">research</a> finding that it improves interpersonal skills in children.</p><p>When Harville Hendrix began marketing mirroring as a beneficial technique for dialoguing couples, it became more utilized by therapists. In his book \"<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Couples-Companion-Meditations-Exercises-Workbook/dp/0671868837\">The Couples Companion: Meditations and Exercises for Getting the Love You Want</a>,\" Hendrix <a href=\"https://books.google.com/books?id=GgVCqUwbmlMC&pg=PA17&lpg=PA17&dq=Mirroring+is+simply+a+matter+of+carefully+repeating+back+what+was+said+for+verification,+and+repeating+the+process+until+we+get+it+right&source=bl&ots=IyX6FihpW8&sig=ACfU3U2T5wqB7o64n03rbtzCUubonqsr_g&hl=en&sa=X&ved=2ahUKEwiotJ_C6r_nAhUXmnIEHbtEA5AQ6AEwAHoECAUQAQ#v=onepage&q=Mirroring%20is%20simply%20a%20matter%20of%20carefully%20repeating%20back%20what%20was%20said%20for%20verification%2C%20and%20repeating%20the%20process%20until%20we%20get%20it%20right&f=false%20until%20we%20get%20it%20right&#38;f=false\">writes</a>, \"Mirroring is simply a matter of carefully repeating back what was said for verification, and repeating the process until we get it right.\"</p><p>With two teenage daughters and many surly mornings, my mother wisely employed mirroring as a way to make her children feel heard. During a time in my life when I often felt misunderstood, listening to my mother reflect my feelings helped to defuse my anger. And when my sister and I fought, mirroring each other paved the way to a mutual understanding.</p><p>\"Mirroring is the best way for two people to resolve conflict,\" my mom would say, as I rolled my eyes in typical teenage fashion.</p><p>It wasn't until I was in a long-term partnership that I discovered she had been right all along.</p><p>Married for five years — and together for much longer — my husband and I are well matched. We make each other laugh, we enjoy the same activities, and we love each other very much. Despite all of this, we are far from perfect. Every relationship has its ups and downs, and during a recent down point, it seemed we were fighting way too often.</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-leaders-track-manage-employee-performance-remotely\">How to best manage your employees' performance remotely — without coming off as a micromanager</a></em></p><p>One evening, a minor dispute morphed into a full-fledged argument. The initial disagreement — which was unbelievably stupid — was blown out of proportion. An hour into our altercation, with no truce in sight, my mom's voice echoed in my head. <em>Try mirroring</em>, the voice said. <em>It's the only way to resolve an argument.</em></p><p>Sitting on the couch opposite my husband, I explained how mirroring worked. Taking turns, each of us would speak in clear sentences, sharing our feelings. The other would listen with care and then repeat the words back verbatim, changing the personal pronouns as needed.</p><p>\"I feel hurt that you don't like our Christmas tree ornaments, because I feel they're an important symbol of our relationship.\" (I told you it was unbelievably stupid.)</p><p>\"You feel hurt that I don't like our Christmas tree ornaments, because you feel they're an important symbol of our relationship.\"</p><p>We continued this back-and-forth rhythm until I felt sufficiently heard, at which point it became my husband's turn to share. To my surprise, he articulated his emotions with a depth of feeling that was uncharacteristic of him.</p><p>Later, when I spoke to my mother about this incident, she wasn't surprised. \"It just takes one person to start mirroring, and if you're willing to <em>really</em> listen, all of a sudden it starts the process.\"</p><p>Her words rang with accuracy. During our argument, I was too invested in my wounded ego to listen to my husband. I had completely shut out his feelings in favor of my own. But mirroring had allowed him to speak and forced me to listen, and vice versa. The result was something truly wonderful: We finally understood each other. Our anger dissipated. The next weekend, we spent an entire day hand-crafting Christmas ornaments, so the tree could reflect more of my husband's taste. It ended up being one of the best days of the year.</p><p>To this day, my mom holds the firm belief that mirroring is the best way to resolve an argument.</p><p>\"Mirroring works because when a normal person is listening to someone else, they're already planning their rebuttal,\" she said. \"But if you have to repeat what the other person says, your brain can't do two things at once. That's the secret of mirroring — it cuts out the planning of your rebuttal so that you can finally hear your spouse.\"</p><p>Though it's a relatively simple concept, it's not as easy as it sounds. For one, it requires a true willingness to listen.</p><p>\"The whole point of mirroring is to listen to the other person, not to get your agenda across. If you want to get your agenda across, don't even do it,\" my mom said.</p><p>She also said that accountability is essential to squashing disagreements. \"Everyone thinks the other person is the problem. Mirroring helps you to understand you're only seeing half of the picture,\" she explained.</p><p>Another important tip? \"If you're in the middle of a big fight, don't mirror right away,\" she said. Heightened emotions may lead to blaming and more squabbling, which means mirroring won't help. After duking it out, make sure to take some time to cool off before starting the process of resolution.</p><p>Which is to say, if you're worried that fighting with your partner means your relationship is doomed, fear not. After working with married couples for 40 years, my mom believes spousal arguments are perfectly natural, healthy even. \"Arguing can be extremely helpful if the argument gets resolved. Personal attacks aren't good, but otherwise, arguments bring festering issues to the surface, which can help the relationship long term,\" she said.</p><p>Mirroring has changed my marriage. After rediscovering this therapy hack, my husband and I no longer quarrel like we used to. When we do find something to disagree on, we mirror each other and find a way to see eye to eye.</p><p>The entire process has revealed recurring patterns in our relationship and allowed us to understand the other's needs. It has taken sacrifices on both our parts, and it's not easy — but we're better off for it. My only regret is not taking my mother's advice sooner.</p><p><em><a href=\"https://jersey-griggs.github.io/\">Jersey Griggs</a> is a writer specializing in lifestyle topics. She lives on the coast of Maine with her husband and their rescue dog. money investors are not comfortable changing their portfolios before certain historic events play out, Deutsche Bank said on Tuesday.</p><p>\"With the <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/index/us-dollar-index\">dollar</a> starting to weaken, many now claim this election outcome is priced in,\" George Saravelos, the bank's head of global foreign exchange research, said of a Biden win and Democratic sweep. \"We disagree.\"</p><p>To establish his point, Saravelos used the <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/eur-usd\">euro-dollar</a> price action earlier this year as an example. The <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/coronavirus-stimulus-eu-recovery-fund-agree-historic-860-billion-plan-2020-7-1029413313#\">European Union had struck a deal in July to borrow billions</a> for the first time in history. The landmark deal, aimed at reconstruction of the bloc, was agreed after days of negotiations. The dollar remained under pressure as the euro rose to a 1-1/2 year high.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f982fa24743a3001216bdf0?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Screenshot 2020 10 27 at 14.32.08\" height=\"734\" width=\"998\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Deutsche Bank</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>\"Even though it was becoming increasingly apparent that an agreement was coming, the euro only rallied after final confirmation of a deal,\" he explained in a note Tuesday. \"The market – especially real money investors – did not feel comfortable changing allocations before such a historic event was out of the way.\"</p><p>\"The same goes for the US election: it is of such historical importance that a shift towards a new approach in trade/foreign policy and<strong><em>&#160;</em></strong>potentially bigger twin deficits will take many weeks to be priced in,\" Saravelos wrote.</p><p><strong data-stringify-type=\"bold\"><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">Read more:</em></strong><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">&#160;</em><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tesla-electric-vehicle-stock-picks-to-buy-bullish-cases-analysts-2020-10?r=US&IR=TIR=T\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-stringify-link=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tesla-electric-vehicle-stock-picks-to-buy-bullish-cases-analysts-2020-10?r=US&IR=TIR=T\" data-sk=\"tooltip_parent\">'EVs are REALLY profitable': Morgan Stanley analyst Adam Jonas and 3 more experts lay out their bullish cases for Tesla and 3 other popular electric-car stocks</a></em></p><p>If President Donald Trump remains in office, that may still lead to a reversal of some recent trends. But by the way investors are placing their bets, Saravelos argues that the 10% risk premium on Trump is so large that there may be \"plenty of room for the dollar to weaken\" if Biden wins.</p><p>A \"risk premium\" is the minimum amount of excess return, above the risk-free rate<wbr>, that an investor requires to take on a certain level of risk.</p><p>The dollar could decline particularly against emerging market currencies, he said. This is where positioning is the lightest right now, and would offer relative growth drivers for investors, he said.&#160;</p><p><strong data-stringify-type=\"bold\"><em And if you're looking for a fresh-air winter adventure, this is a great year to try one (or more) of Colorado's 28 <a href=\"https://www.colorado.com/activities/colorado-skiing\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">world-class ski resorts</a>. Below, we detail our top picks for the best ski resorts in Colorado, plus the best hotel in each area, including:</p><ul class=\"summary-list\"><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-ski-resorts-colorado/#crested-butte-1\">Crested Butte</a></li><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-ski-resorts-colorado/#breckenridge-3\">Breckenridge</a></li><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-ski-resorts-colorado/#steamboat-springs-5\">Steamboat Springs</a></li><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-ski-resorts-colorado/#silverton-mountain-7\" rel=\"noopener\">Silverton Mountain</a></li><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-ski-resorts-colorado/#aspen-snowmass-9\">Aspen Snowmass</a></li><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-ski-resorts-colorado/#telluride-11\">Telluride</a></li><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-ski-resorts-colorado/#winter-park-resort-13\">Winter Park</a></li><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-ski-resorts-colorado/#vail-15\">Vail</a></li></ul><p>All of the ski areas have introduced new COVID-related safety precautions in coordination with the Colorado Department of Public Health and Environment, so it's a good idea to check each resort's specific policies. We've included links to that information for the eight resorts we've listed below. Check Colorado's statewide <a href=\"https://covid19.colorado.gov/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">COVID-19 updates</a> for additional details on infection rates, testing sites, and the recently renewed mandatory <a href=\"https://covid19.colorado.gov/mask-guidance\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">mask-wearing requirement</a>.</p><p>Some of the common changes for the 2020-2021 ski season include requiring face coverings, physical distancing (including on chairlifts and in gondolas), advance reservations for lift tickets (often granting priority to pass holders), cashless transactions, limiting class size for lessons, and reducing restaurant seating. Many resorts are also limiting on-mountain capacity, especially for peak dates so it may pay off to plan and book early.&#160;</p><p>While outdoor recreation is relatively safe, it's important to consider the risks of&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/is-travel-safe-coronavirus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">travel</a>&#160;in general, and of staying in&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/are-hotels-safe-coronavirus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">hotels</a>. Without a vaccine, there is no guarantee of safety, and we recommend following guidelines put forward by organizations like the CDC and WHO, such as always wearing a mask, washing hands frequently, and practicing social distancing.</p><p>Additionally, just because an activity is outside doesn't mean it's safe and it's important to weigh the risk factors of skiing and snowboarding, such as potentially encountering crowded areas like lift lines and lodging areas. Aspen Mountain's 675 acres are accessible directly from downtown Aspen, and 470-acre Buttermilk may be known as the home of the X Games but it's also a great place for beginners and families with kids.</p><p>Read the Aspen Snowmass <a href=\"https://www.aspensnowmass.com/plan-your-stay/tickets-and-passes/~/link.aspx?_id=6AB1BD19E2DA42039525B46B89BD929F&#38;_z=z\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">COVID-19 update for the season</a>.</p><p><strong>Opening day:</strong> Aspen Mountain and Snowmass open November 26; Aspen Highlands opens December 12; Buttermilk is opening December 18.</p>\n\tWhere to stay in Aspen Snowmass: The Gant Aspen\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f9713af4743a3001216baf5?format=jpeg\" alt=\"best ski hotels colorado gant aspen\" height=\"853\" width=\"1137\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Booking.com</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=6776&#38;awinaffid=257137&#38;clickref=&#38;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fhotel%2Fus%2Fthe-gant.en-gb.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Book The Gant Aspen starting at $236 per night</a></h2><p>Located in a quiet area of downtown, The Gant is a five-acre condominium resort that offers spacious accommodations and homey amenities within a short shuttle ride of the Silver Queen Gondola that glides to the top of Aspen Mountain.</p><p>On-site Ski Butlers can bring rental gear directly to your condo for private fittings. The resort concierge can help with lift tickets and lesson reservations (you can let them know with an online request in advance), and when you're done with the day's excitement, you can soak in one of the hotel's three hot tubs or two outdoor pools.</p><p>Pepperjack's Caf&#233; offers breakfast and lunch, plus coffee, local craft beer, and cocktails, with dine-in, take-out, or room delivery options.</p><p>The ever-circulating Gant Vans offer free in-town and airport shuttle service, and you can even schedule a pick-up by using a new Gant App. If you're driving yourself, the hotel offers free parking, with two Tesla charging stations.</p><p>A range of condominiums are available, from standard to deluxe to premier level, sized from one- to four-bedrooms. All have wood-burning fireplaces, full kitchens, humidifiers, a washer/dryer, balconies, and free Wi-Fi. The premier units have been professionally decorated, with the latest mountain modern d&#233;cor and furnishings, plus upgraded appliances and linens.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.tripadvisor.com/Hotel_Review-g29141-d82770-Reviews-The_Gant-Aspen_Colorado.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\"><strong>Trip Advisor</strong></a><strong> Ranking:</strong> 4 out of 34 hotels in Aspen</p><p><a class=\"copyright\">Telluride Ski Resort</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>In Western Colorado's San Juan Mountains, <a href=\"https://www.tellurideskiresort.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Telluride Ski Resort</a> takes advantage of its steep canyon setting and includes 148 trails weaving through 2,000 acres. Although nearly 60% of Telluride is beginner- and intermediate-friendly, the resort also takes pride in its extreme hike-to terrain that challenges experts with steep chutes, cliffs, and deep powder.&#160;</p><p>Read Telluride's <a href=\"https://www.tellurideskiresort.com/the-mountain/knowb4ugo/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">COVID-19 update for the season</a>.</p><p><strong>Opening day:</strong> November 26</p>\n\tWhere to stay in Telluride: The Inn at Lost Creek\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f9715674743a3001216bafd?format=jpeg\" alt=\"the inn at lost creek\" height=\"505\" width=\"674\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Trip Advisor</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.hotels.com/ho202280/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Book The Inn at Lost Creek starting at $289 per night</a></h2><p>Tucked into the base of the canyon, the tiny town of Telluride is a National Historic District with an enticing mix of shops, galleries, and restaurants. There's a free gondola that lifts passengers up to Mountain Village in 13 minutes, and that's where you'll find <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.hotels.com/ho202280/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow sponsored\">The Inn at Lost Creek</a>, a quick glide from the gondola station. Mountain Village, at 9,500 feet, is a modern counterpart to Telluride, with an open-air plaza often filled with live music, plus cafes, restaurants, and shops.</p><p>The Inn at Lost Creek is a ski-in/ski-out boutique hotel with mountain lodge d&#233;cor accented by wood and stone, furnished comfortably in soft textures and colors for a warm, casual vibe. The Ski Valet and Boot Lounge takes the trouble out of juggling all your winter gear. Their ski valets will set your skis outside in the rack for you, and store your gear and dry your boots overnight. They also arrange rentals through Christy's Sports on request.</p><p>The hotel's 32 units range from a 400-square-foot Queen-bed studio with a kitchenette, to a 1,000-square-foot, two-bedroom condo with a full kitchen, gas fireplace, and steam shower. All have a jetted tub, balcony, washer/dryer, humidifier, 450-thread-count Pratesi linens with a feather duvet, plus robes and slippers.</p><p>A free, cooked-to-order breakfast is served daily, and Siam's Talay Grille is located on-site. Two rooftop hot tubs provide blissful mountain views, and guests also have access to the nearby Spa at The Peaks Resort.&#160;</p><p><a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.tripadvisor.com/Hotel_Review-g2004180-d119910-Reviews-The_Inn_at_Lost_Creek-Mountain_Village_Colorado.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\"><strong>Trip Advisor</strong></a> <strong>Ranking:</strong> 1 out of 7 hotels in Mountain Village</p><p><a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.hotels.com/ho202280/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\"><strong>Hotels.com</strong></a><strong> Rating:</strong> 9.8 out of 10</p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Guests praise the friendly staff, the ideal location, and the dog-friendly attitude.</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Valet parking is $20 per night, and reservations are required to use the hot tubs.</p><p><strong>COVID-19 status and policies: </strong>The hotel opens for the winter season on November 26. Please contact them directly for new procedures.</p>\n\tWinter Park Resort\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f9716c0f21803001222c006?format=jpeg\" alt=\"2019 wp charlesstemen dsc08437 dng\" height=\"1350\" width=\"1800\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Winter Park Resort</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>USA Today readers named <a href=\"https://www.winterparkresort.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Winter Park</a> the #1 Ski Resort in North America for two years in a row, and it's easy to see why it's a popular favorite. Only 67 miles northwest of Denver, Winter Park offers 3,081 skiable acres, with 23 lifts and 166 trails.</p><p>Skiers and snowboarders will find variety here: groomed runs, glades, bowls, tree skiing, backcountry, moguls, and a terrain park with 80 different features and an 18-foot superpipe. If you feel like a change from downhill skiing, Devil's Thumb also boasts 75 miles of Nordic ski trails.</p><p>Still not enough action? The ranch offers a game room with a two-lane bowling alley (available by reservation), an outdoor ice-skating rink, and a 37-seat movie theater. Heck's Tavern offers gourmet casual food, while the more upscale Ranch House Restaurant &#38; Saloon (currently closed, but expected to reopen for Christmas) focuses on New American Mountain Cuisine.</p><p>The decor is rustic Americana ranch with an elegant touch. There's a warm cabin vibe with lots of knotty wood, leather armchairs, plush cushions, quilts, and rag rugs.</p><p>Main Lodge rooms include King, King Suite, King with fireplace, Double Queen, and Two Queen with fireplace. High Lonesome Lodge rooms include King, King with fireplace, King with sitting area, King Suite, Lofted King Suite (the loft includes a Queen bed and &#190; bath), and Double Queen. The seven 1,050-square-foot, two-bedroom cabins have two king beds, a \"modified kitchen\" and a wood-burning fireplace. Two four-bedroom cabins offer 2,200 square feet, with two king beds, two queen beds, two bathrooms, a full kitchen, and a dining area. For big groups, Devil's Thumb also offers two private guest houses just off the property: Peak-to-Peak Ranch sleeps eight, and the 10,000-square-foot Grand Guest House sleeps up to 14.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.tripadvisor.com/Hotel_Review-g33666-d142175-Reviews-Devil_s_Thumb_Ranch_Resort_Spa-Tabernash_Grand_County_Colorado.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\"><strong>Trip Advisor</strong></a><strong> Ranking</strong><strong>:</strong> 1 out of 1 hotel in Tabernash</p><p><strong>Booking.com Rating:</strong> Not yet rated</p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>The staff are friendly, the ranch activities are plentiful, and the peaceful vibe is relaxing. The on-site Bloom Spa offers CBD-infused massage therapies and high-altitude adjustment treatments, and the outdoor terrace features a heated pool, four hot tubs, and a fire pit.</p><p>One great perk of The Sebastian is their Base Camp, a cozy little private club right next to Gondola One, where ski valets can help you with equipment rentals, store your gear, and even serve you cookies and hot cocoa when you need a warm-up.</p><p>Rooms at The Sebastian range from a Queen classic to a four-bedroom residential suite. src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f98008af21803001222c23e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Donald Trump, Trump\" height=\"457\" width=\"914\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">AP Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul><li><strong>The S&#38;P 500 could rally about 14% to hit 3,900 if President Donald Trump wins the November election, according to JPMorgan.</strong></li><li><strong>A Trump victory is the \"most favorable outcome for equities,\" a team of analysts led by the chief US equity strategist Dubravko Lakos-Bujas said in a note on Friday.</strong></li><li><strong>They said a \"Blue Sweep\" scenario would be mostly neutral for equities in the short term, because more federal stimulus could be offset by rising corporate taxes.</strong></li><li><strong>JPMorgan said it expected energy, financials, and healthcare to see the biggest moves, as both Joe Biden and Trump mentioned the sectors specifically on their campaign trails.</strong></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</strong></li></ul><hr><p>The <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/index/s&p_500_500\">S&#38;P 500</a> could rise 14%, to 3,900, if President Donald Trump retains his position in the White House, JPMorgan analysts said on Friday.</p><p>A Trump victory could push the mega-cap index 300 points higher than the firm's base-case target for year-end, the analysts said. The S&#38;P 500 stood at about 3,400 at Monday's close.</p><p>Markets have been <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/markets-outlook-biden-election-victory-democratic-senate-fiscal-stimulus-jpmorgan-2020-10-1029694606#\">preparing for a Democratic sweep and frontloaded stimulus</a> to boost the economic recovery. But JPMorgan analysts led by Dubravko Lakos-Bujas, the chief US equity strategist, said they expected \"an 'orderly' Trump victory as the most favorable outcome for equities.\"</p><p>On the other hand, \"a 'Blue Sweep' scenario is expected to be mostly neutral in the short term, as it would likely be accompanied by some immediate positive catalysts (i.e. larger fiscal stimulus / infrastructure) but also negative catalysts (i.e. rising corporate taxes),\" the team wrote.</p><p>JPMorgan said that after analyzing Twitter sentiment and comparing it with traditional polling data, it found more evidence that the race was tightening, while traders seemed to be minimizing the risk of a contested election.</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/stock-picks-to-buy-companies-beat-q3-earnings-expectations-bofa-2020-10\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">BANK OF AMERICA: Buy these 11 underowned stocks ahead of their earnings reports because they're the most likely candidates to beat expectations in the weeks ahead</a></em></p><p>The bank said it expected the energy, financials, and healthcare sectors to see the biggest price swings, as both Trump and Joe Biden, the Democratic nominee, referred to them on their campaign trails.</p><p>JPMorgan has created baskets of stocks that bet on winners from either Democratic or Republican victories in November. A glance at the top components of both baskets showed that the Biden basket, including alternative-energy and green-tech stocks, was outperforming the Trump basket, with traditional energy and fossil-fuel companies, by 66%.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f98092bf21803001222c24f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Screenshot 2020 10 27 at 11.48.05\" height=\"942\" width=\"1064\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">JPMorgan</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>\"Given the large divergence between these two baskets (i.e. similar to momentum/value), coupled with our expectation that COVID-19 headline risk likely declines post-election, we see an increasingly compelling case for Value in the coming period,\" the analysts said.</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/chamath-palihapitiya-shares-5-sectors-shaping-long-term-investing-plan-2020-10\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">'I'm basically going to be long growth': Billionaire investor Chamath Palihapitiya has hauled in a 997% return since 2011. and UNESCO reporting over 11 million girls may not go back to school after the COVID-19 crisis, the scale of the challenge is immense, the study said.<br><br>However, this also presents an In fact, the Supreme Court has <a href=\"https://constitution.congress.gov/\">overruled</a> almost 300 of its own decisions since its inception.&#160;</p><p>Grainger says that should the court go that far, there would be \"revolt.\"</p><p>\"I think we are seeing now a population that is tired of oppression,\" she said. \"We're seeing that with the racial justice uprisings. I think we'd see something very similar around Roe.\"</p><p>Roe has been challenged several times, and Barrett's mentor, Justice Antonin Scalia, was in favor of overturning it, his son Christopher Scalia told Business Insider.</p><p>\"My father thought that the Supreme Court had no business declaring that that was a constitutional right when the Constitution is silent on abortion,\" he said. \"So my father's point wasn't that abortion should be banned nationally. My father's point was that the Constitution is silent on that, meaning it's left in the hands of states to make those decisions.\"&#160;</p><p>Justice Antonin Scalia was on the opposite end of the ideological spectrum from <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/supreme-court-justice-ruth-bader-ginsburg-has-died-2019-8\">Justice Ruth Bader Ginsburg</a>, who fought for women's rights. But at the end of the day, they were still good friends. Scalia's son says that if that collegiality is lost the court will suffer.</p><p>\"I don't know that it necessarily means that opinions will suddenly be shoddy or anything like that,\" he said. \"But I think that one of the things that sets the court apart is that collegiality. And I think that one of the reasons Americans trust the Supreme Court and the judicial branch generally more than the other branches of government is because they sense that collegiality.</p><p>But Grainger says that with Republicans rushing Barrett to the bench just weeks after Ginsburg's death, the court has already taken a political turn.</p><p>\"I am a lawyer who believes in the courts and believes in the history of the court of how it has protected and advanced rights for oppressed people,\" she said. \"But I do think now it's very hard to ignore that the court is becoming a political body.\"</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/amy-coney-barrett-supreme-court-issues-roe-wade-2020-10'>Business alt=\"samsung event cox 6\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2222\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Your Android settings may be forcing your incoming calls to go directly to voicemail.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Crystal Cox/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Incoming calls on your Android may go straight to voicemail for several reasons, including issues with your phone's SIM card or its Bluetooth and Do Not Disturb settings.&#160;</li>\n<li>There are five quick and easy ways you can troubleshoot when your calls are going straight to voicemail.&#160;</li>\n<li>If none of these fixes work, you should reach out to your cellular service provider for assistance.&#160;</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\">Visit Business Insider's Tech Reference library for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Incoming calls on your Android phone inexplicably going straight to voicemail without ringing is a mundane — yet frustrating — issue. But there is an explanation and, more importantly, a way to fix it.&#160;</p><p>While there could be several possible causes, almost all of them involve your phone's settings, making it generally easy to troubleshoot. Among the handful of things that might automatically send your calls to voicemail is your phone's Do Not Disturb mode, blocked numbers, call forwarding, Bluetooth connections, and your phone's SIM card.&#160;</p><p>Whether you accidentally activated any of these phone features or forgot you turned them on, don't fret. Restoring your Android's default settings to receive calls again can be a quick process.&#160;&#160;</p><h2>How to troubleshoot your Android when incoming calls go straight to voicemail</h2><p>Here are five things to troubleshoot when your calls go straight to voicemail — and the one thing you should do when nothing else works.&#160;</p><h3><strong>Turn off your Android's Do Not Disturb mode</strong></h3><p>If your phone is set to \"<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/do-not-disturb-android\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Do Not Disturb</a>,\" most or all of your phone calls will go directly to voicemail. So it's worth checking to see if the phone has been accidentally put in that mode.&#160;</p><p><strong>1.</strong> Pull down your phone's Control Center by swiping down from the top of the screen.&#160;</p><p><strong>2.</strong> Check that the Do Not Disturb icon is not enabled.&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f9346d9f21803001222bbef?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Why_does_my_Android_go_straight_to_voicemail 1\" height=\"3040\" width=\"1440\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Make sure Do Not Disturb isn&#39;t enabled.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Dave Johnson/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>For more information, read our article \"<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/do-not-disturb-android\">How to turn on and customize Do Not Disturb settings on your Android phone</a>.\"</p><h3><strong>Remove a number from your blocked numbers list on Android</strong></h3><p>Are you using your phone's call blocking feature? It can come in handy to stop telemarketers and other unwanted calls, but you might be <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-block-a-number-on-android\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">accidentally blocking phone numbers</a> that you want to ring through. You can turn this off in your Android Phone app.&#160;</p><p><strong>1.</strong> Start the Phone app.&#160;</p><p><strong>2.</strong> Tap the three dots at the top of the screen.&#160;</p><p><strong>3.</strong> In the drop-down menu, choose \"Settings.\"&#160;</p><p><strong>4.</strong> Select \"Block numbers.\"&#160;</p><p><strong>5.</strong> Remove any phone numbers from the list you don't want to send to voicemail immediately.&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f9346f54743a3001216b709?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Why does my Android go straight to voicemail 2\" height=\"3040\" width=\"1440\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Blocked phone numbers go straight to voicemail.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Dave Johnson/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>For more details, read our article \"<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-block-a-number-on-android\">How to block a number on any Android phone to stop receiving unwanted calls</a>.\"</p><h3><strong>Disable any call forwarding features</strong></h3><p>Not all Android phones support call forwarding, and it depends on your cellular provider, but you may be forwarding your calls directly to your voicemail or another number. Disabling any of your Android device's call forwarding features may resolve the issue.&#160;</p><p><strong>1.</strong> Start the Phone app.</p><p><strong>2.</strong> Tap the three dots in the top left of the screen.&#160;</p><p><strong>3.</strong> Select \"Settings\" or \"Call Settings.\"</p><p><strong>4.</strong> Choose \"Calls.\"</p><p><strong>5.</strong> Tap \"Call forwarding.\"&#160;</p><p><strong>6.</strong> Turn off any of the four listed options: \"Always forward,\" \"Forward when busy,\" \"Forward when unanswered,\" and \"Forward when unreached.\"</p><h3><strong>Turn your Bluetooth connection off&#160;</strong></h3><p>Sometimes, your phone's Bluetooth connection can get confused and think it's connected to a device when, in fact, it's not. You might have experienced this when you turn off Bluetooth earbuds, and audio does not switch to the phone's speaker. Instead, all you hear is silence. Luckily, the remedy is simple.&#160;</p><p><strong>1.</strong> Pull down the Control Center by swiping down from the top of the screen.&#160;</p><p><strong>2.</strong> Tap the Bluetooth icon to turn it off completely.&#160;</p><p><strong>3.</strong> Wait a moment and then tap it again to turn it back on.&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f9347104743a3001216b70a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Why_does_my_Android_go_straight_to_voicemail 3\" height=\"3040\" width=\"1440\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Toggle your Bluetooth connection to see if that solves the problem.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Dave Johnson/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h3><strong>Replace your Android phone's SIM card</strong></h3><p>Sometimes, a faulty or damaged SIM card can cause weird problems, and it's more likely to be the culprit if you remove and replace the SIM card often. In other words, the more you handle it, the more likely it's a problem.&#160;</p><p>You can attempt to remove, reseat, and insert the SIM card to address the issue. But to be 100 percent sure it's the reason your calls are going straight to voicemail, you should contact your cellular provider and replace the card with a new version. You can request a new SIM card without changing your phone number or making any changes to your service.&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f93484a4743a3001216b712?format=jpeg\" alt=\"A woman putting a SIM card in her phone\" height=\"1412\" width=\"1883\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A woman putting the sim card from her phone on a table.\n<p class=\"copyright\">AntonioGuillem/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h3><strong>Check your coverage and talk to your cellular provider</strong></h3><p>If none of those simple fixes solved your problem, it's more likely that the problem is not with your Android handset but with your cellular service.&#160;</p><p>Try looking at a coverage map from your provider to see if you have reliable service or test your service with another phone. If your coverage is very weak, incoming calls can go straight to voicemail. You can also try calling your cellular provider's customer service for additional troubleshooting support.&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f9347694743a3001216b70b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Why_does_my_Android_go_straight_to_voicemail 4\" height=\"1616\" width=\"2174\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Check a coverage map to see if your home or office is in a dead zone.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Dave Johnson/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h2>Related coverage from&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\">Tech Reference</a>:</h2><ul><li><h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/why-wont-my-bluetooth-connect\">'Why won't my Bluetooth device REUTERS/Aly Song\" height=\"2782\" width=\"5565\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A Xilinx sign is seen during the China International Import Expo (CIIE), at the National Exhibition and Convention Center in Shanghai\n<p class=\"copyright\">Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul><li><strong><a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/xlnx-stock\">Xilinx</a> shares soared as much as 14% higher on Tuesday after <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/amd-stock\">Advanced Micro Devices</a> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amd-buying-xilinx-in-all-stock-deal-valued-at-35b-2020-10\">agreed to buy the company in a $35 billion deal</a>.</strong></li><li><strong>The acquisition is expected to close by the end of 2021, according to a <a href=\"https://www.amd.com/en/press-releases/2020-10-27-amd-to-acquire-xilinx-creating-the-industry-s-high-performance-computing\">press release</a>. Xilinx shareholders will receive 1.7234 shares of AMD for each Xilinx share they own.</strong></li><li><strong>The combined entity will boast more than 13,000 engineers and give AMD a major leg-up in the communications technology business, particularly against rival firm <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/intc-stock\">Intel</a>.</strong></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/xlnx-stock\">Watch Xilinx trade live here</a>.</strong></li></ul><hr><p><a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/xlnx-stock\">Xilinx</a> surged as much as 14% on Tuesday&#160;after <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/amd-stock\">Advanced Micro Devices</a> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amd-buying-xilinx-in-all-stock-deal-valued-at-35b-2020-10\">agreed to buy the chipmaker for $35 billion</a>.</p><p>The deal is expected to close by the end of 2021, according to a <a href=\"https://www.amd.com/en/press-releases/2020-10-27-amd-to-acquire-xilinx-creating-the-industry-s-high-performance-computing\">press release</a>. AMD's all-stock purchase will grant current Xilinx shareholders 1.7234 shares of AMD for each Xilinx share they own.&#160;Current AMD shareholders will own 74% of the new company, while Xilinx investors will own the remaining 26%.</p><p>The combined entity will boast more than 13,000 engineers and help both firms compete with lagging industry titan <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/intc-stock\">Intel</a>. AMD also expects to unlock roughly $300 million worth of operational efficiencies through the deal over the next 18 months.</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/european-value-stock-picks-to-buy-avoid-outpeformance-bofa-2020-10\" data-analytics-position=\"2\" data-analytics-module=\"\">BANK OF AMERICA: Buy these 22 European value stocks to cash in on a possible 10% rally in early 2021 — but avoid these 6 'value traps'</a></em></p><p>Still, AMD shares fell as much as 4.9% in Tuesday trading.</p><p>Xilinx similarly rallied on October 9 after <a href=\"https://www.wsj.com/articles/amd-is-in-advanced-talks-to-buy-xilinx-11602205553\">The Wall Street Journal</a> first reported on the potential AMD deal. The leap placed shares at their highest point since July 2019. &#160;</p><p>The acquisition is the latest mega-deal to hit the semiconductor sector this year. It dwarfs <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/adi-stock?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestgest\">Analog Devices'</a> purchase of <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/mxim-stock?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestgest\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Maxim Integrated Products</a> for $20 billion and falls just short of tying <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/nvda-stock?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestgest\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Nvidia</a> $40 billion takeover of Arm Holdings.</p><p>Xilinx produces chips used in data centers and 5G base stations, giving AMD a major leg-up in the communications technology business. It also alleviates some concerns around future revenue. Xilinx shares tumbled through 2019 after US-China trade tensions limited shipments from Huawei. The Chinese tech giant accounts for 8% of Xilinx's revenue.</p><p>Xilinx closed at $114.55 per share on Monday, up about 17% year-to-date.</p><p>AMD closed at $82.23, up roughly 81% year-to-date.</p><p><em><strong>Now read more markets coverage from Markets Insider and Business Insider:</strong></em></p><p><em><strong><a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/earnings-season-tech-bubble-trend-perverse-stock-market-reactions-bofa-2020-10-1029722185\" data-analytics-position=\"3\" data-analytics-module=\"\">Earnings season is repeating a tech-bubble trend filled with counterintuitive market reactions, Bank of America says</a></strong></em></p><p><em><strong><a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/stock-market-outlook-capital-gains-tax-temporary-hurdle-biden-goldman-2020-10-1029721773\" data-analytics-position=\"4\" data-analytics-module=\"\">A capital-gains tax hike would only temporarily slow the stock market's rally, Goldman Sachs says</a></strong></em></p><p><em><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/chamath-palihapitiya-shares-5-sectors-shaping-long-term-investing-plan-2020-10\" data-analytics-position=\"8\" data-analytics-module=\"\">'I'm basically going to be long growth': Billionaire investor Chamath Palihapitiya has hauled in a 997% return since 2011. Settings are pretty minimal aside from a popcorn button, a frozen setting, and a coffee setting, so you won't have to experiment with too many features that may or may not actually cook your food the way you want. Simply set your cook time and walk away or add 30-second intervals with one touch.</p><p>I've had an earlier version of this microwave for the better part of a decade, at least, and have yet to come across a single issue. While I don't use the microwave all that often, others in the household rely almost exclusively&#160;upon it.</p><p><strong>Pros:&#160;</strong>Powerful, well-priced</p><p><strong>Cons:&#160;</strong>The warranty and associated customer service may be lacking</p>\n\tThe best over-the-range microwave\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f3559d4b4bb1c001df530c6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"best microwave\" height=\"600\" width=\"800\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Walmart</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><strong><a href=\"http://bestbuy.7tiv.net/c/196318/614286/10014?subId1=biipg_071118_best-microwaves&#38;u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bestbuy.com%2Fsite%2Fwhirlpool-1-9-cu-ft-convection-over-the-range-microwave-with-sensor-cooking-fingerprint-resistant-stainless-steel%2F5900303.p%3FskuId%3D5900303\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow\">Whirlpool's 1.9-cubic-foot Convection Over-the-Range Microwave</a>&#160;is easy to install, has a sensor that adjusts cooking time and power based on the weight of your dish, and comes with a powerful blower to&#160;whisk steam and smoke from your kitchen.</strong></h3><p>Over-the-range microwaves are more permanent installations than countertop models, and they're also taking the place of a range hood so we think they're worth spending a little more money. It&#160;includes a four-speed, 400-cubic-foot-per-minute (cfm) blower that should handle even the heaviest of steams and smokes.</p><p><a href=\"http://bestbuy.7tiv.net/c/196318/614286/10014?subId1=biipg_071118_best-microwaves&#38;u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bestbuy.com%2Fsite%2Fwhirlpool-1-9-cu-ft-convection-over-the-range-microwave-with-sensor-cooking-fingerprint-resistant-stainless-steel%2F5900303.p%3FskuId%3D5900303\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow\">Whirlpool's Over-the-Range Convection Microwave</a> is equipped for \"scan-to-cook\" technology so that you can scan a food item's barcode with your phone and send its cooking instructions directly to your microwave. It also offers steam control and sensor cooking to prevent overcooking. The convection rack is a nice, unique touch that lets you heat multiple items at once, and the large 14-inch turntable should accommodate almost any dish you'd use in the microwave.</p><p>Because this is a convection oven, you can easily get away with cooking most dishes in the microwave, even if your aim is to brown or crisp your cuisine.</p><p>Whirlpool also has a \"SteamClean\" technology that steams and loosens particles so all you have to do is give a quick wipe with the sponge &#8212; a much easier cleaning job than with other microwaves. While you can do this simply enough by microwaving a bowl of water and wiping the microwave clean, it's more convenient to save yourself the step.</p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Optional convection rack, steam cleaning, sleek design with backlit controls that only turn on when in use</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Automatic fan can be annoying, may have Wi-Fi connectivity issues&#160;</p>\n\tThe best built-in microwave\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f356a3ae89ebf001f044543?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Panasonic NN SD975S Microwave Lifestyle\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B010RWYPBK/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipg_071118_best-microwaves-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B010RWYPBK&#38;linkId=ea524ffef13b96fb15af19172e9cbfb2\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Panasonic's NN-SD975S Microwave</a> is powerful, featuring unique cyclonic inverter technology, but it's still compact enough that it should fit your cabinet or counter space.&#160;</h3><p>With 1250 watts, this <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B010RWYPBK/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipg_071118_best-microwaves-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B010RWYPBK&#38;linkId=ea524ffef13b96fb15af19172e9cbfb2\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Panasonic</a> is the most powerful microwave on our list, and it's among the more powerful microwaves on the market. Panasonic's patented Inverter technology allows you to steam, braise, and poach, but it also performs more traditional microwave functions. That is to say yes, of course, it will still pop your corn.</p><p>There are 20 preset options that let you easily cook everything from oatmeal to pasta, and many things in between with the simple touch of a button. Meanwhile, the special cyclonic inverter will circulate heat in waves, resulting in more texture, color, and nutrient retention. Delicate foods can also heat up without being overcooked.&#160;</p><p>Regardless of the size you require, the&#160;<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B010RWYPBK/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipg_071118_best-microwaves-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B010RWYPBK&#38;linkId=ea524ffef13b96fb15af19172e9cbfb2\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Panasonic NN-SD975S</a> has more space on the inside than most microwaves, thanks to the inverter, which kicks out more power than a machine of this size usually would. Its 16.5-inch turntable tray will accommodate large plates, too.</p><p>This microwave works as both a countertop unit and as a built-in. Affordable, fool-proof, small, dials instead of electronic buttons</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Maybe too small for some and not enough presets for others</p>\n\tThe best convection microwave\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f355be6e89ebf001f0444ed?format=jpeg\" alt=\"best microwave 3\" height=\"600\" width=\"800\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2zpO45z\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"></a><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B071ZSCY1P/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipg_071118_best-microwaves-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B076V5DJ4S&#38;linkId=fead49e14075a0c8d0dc605c0d4bdbfa&#38;th=1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Toshiba EC042A5C-SS</a>&#160;is a convection oven without the hefty price tag of other microwaves.</h3><p>If you're not going to invest in a microwave with an inverter, but you still want something that's suitable for more than just cooking Cup of Noodles or reheating coffee, then consider a convection oven, which will also even out the heat and keep&#160;the edges and center of your dish from burning.</p><p>The&#160;<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B071ZSCY1P/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipg_071118_best-microwaves-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B076V5DJ4S&#38;linkId=fead49e14075a0c8d0dc605c0d4bdbfa&#38;th=1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Toshiba EC042A5C-SS</a> isn't exactly cheap, by any means, but we don't think it's completely out of the question if you're looking for a good microwave that can handle heating most foods. Like with most things, the less you spend on a microwave upfront, the sooner you'll end up having to replace it anyhow.</p><p>More to that point, there are more than enough online reviews about microwaves shorting out and bursting into flames than even we have time to read, and that's enough to scare us into spending a little more for some peace of mind in the kitchen.</p><p>With all of its enthusiastic customer reviews and the great price tag, which is about half the going rate for comparable Panasonic and GE microwaves, we're convinced Toshiba is the way to go for a convection microwave.</p><p><strong>Pros:&#160;</strong>Affordable, positive reviews citing positive customer service experiences&#160;</p><p><strong>Cons:&#160;</strong>Might not get quite as hot as other convection microwave ovens</p>\n\tWhat to look for in a microwave\n\t\n\t<p>Here are a few things to keep in mind as you shop.</p><ul><li><strong>Wattage and size:&#160;</strong>Most microwaves pack anywhere from 600 to 1200 watts in power. Larger, more expensive machines cook faster, while smaller, less expensive options will still get hot enough to heat most things. However, they probably won't cook as evenly. Size and wattage usually go hand in hand, but size is its own consideration based on where your microwave will fit.</li><li><strong>Location:&#160;</strong>Countertop microwaves to take up precious space, but when that's all you have to give up, it's your best and only option. Over-the-range models fit over your stove and take the place of a range hood. If you have space, they're great, but they're also usually more expensive. Built-in microwaves can be tucked into a cabinet, but they're probably best for large kitchens where drawer and cabinet space is not at a premium.</li><li><strong>Convection and inverter: </strong>Convection microwave ovens blow air into the microwave so that heat is distributed more evenly, making them the most consistent and reliable option. However, they're usually more expensive. Microwaves with inverters can run at partial power while maintaining an even temperature, while other microwaves just pulse on and off, allowing the temperature to vary. Like convection ovens, inverter microwaves are a little more expensive but worth the extra money if you tend to cook in your microwave a lot or draw butter or chocolate regularly enough.</li><li><strong>Presets and controls:</strong> Many microwaves come with presets, but those can be faulty and add confusion to the interface. I've often opened the microwave after using a preset and found either half-frozen mush or worse still, utter devastation. It's often in your best interest to choose your own time and power settings. We recommend going with short intervals so you don't overheat your food.</li></ul>\n\tWhat we're currently testing\n\t\n\t<p>Here's what we're currently testing for a future update to this guide:</p><ul><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B085SV35MT/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;creativeASIN=B085SV35MT&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;tag=biipg_071118_best-microwaves-20&#38;linkId=0a25d2a61c9c227084cedd5b343bb1c1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Panasonic NN-CD87KS Home Chef</a>:</strong> This is billed as a 4-in-1 unit and works as a &#160;microwave, broiler, air fryer, and convection oven. It's sleek but larger than a standard microwave, so you'll need some extra counter space or a trim kit to build this into your kitchen cabinets.&#160;So far, we've been impressed with its capabilities as a convection oven, but not as a microwave &#8212; the wattage was not powerful enough to microwave popcorn according to the bag's time. We'll continue testing this model over the next few months for a more comprehensive update to the guide.</li></ul>\n\tCheck out our other small appliance buying guides\n\t<figure>\n\t<img The city sets a high bar for accommodations at any price, even for a two-figure price tag — yes, well under $100, and in many cases under $50. New policies include:</p><ul><li>All hotel guests will have their temperature checked prior to check-in.</li><li>In addition to using specialized, CDC recommended disinfectants, the hotel is applying an EPA registered, anti-microbial surface protectant to high-touch items like door handles, gaming chips, elevator buttons, and slot machine panels.</li><li>Complimentary masks are available on property.</li><li>Guest rooms have been thoroughly disinfected with special attention paid to areas of high contact areas.</li><li>Fresh linens are laundered locally to ensure the best quality of cleaning products and proper water temperature. An amenity kit with protective items will be made available to all hotel guests.</li><li>During their stay, guests can use contactless virtual concierge services to request additional amenities, fresh towels, and trash removal.</li><li>Players of live table games will be asked to wear cloth facemasks and to step away from the game if they want to smoke. Guests can expect additional space between slot machines and may request a machine to be sanitized.</li><li>Restaurants have eliminated reusable menus, utilize single-use items, and seating is limited to permit appropriate distance between guests.</li><li>The resort will increase the amount of outside air brought into the ventilation system to \"turn over\" inside air more quickly, and replace air filters on a regular basis.</li><li>Markers will note the distance guests should keep between other people not in their group and smaller areas will limit the number of guests.</li><li>Plexiglass shields will be used and staff will wear masks and undergo temperature checks.</li><li>All pool areas are deep cleaned and the layout will be updated to include social distancing guidelines and proper space between guests.
